	Callback = function(Value)
		auto_message = Value

        end
	end    
})

                })
                wait(305)
            
            for i,v in pairs(getconnections(nextButton.MouseButton1Click)) do
                v:Function()
            end

            wait(2)

            nameButton.Text = art_name

            wait(2)

            for i,v in pairs(getconnections(finishButton.MouseButton1Click)) do
            v:Function()
            end   
            end
        end
    end
})


-- _____________ REQUIRED _____________ --
OrionLib:Init()
